## Top 5 critical issues

- /legal @ 360×740: horizontal-scroll (html, body)
- /legal @ 375×667: horizontal-scroll (html, body)
- /legal @ 390×844: horizontal-scroll (html, body)

## Recommended fix order

1) Eliminate horizontal scroll + overflow sources (layout containment + responsive containers)
2) Fix tap target sizing for primary nav + all CTAs and form controls (44×44 minimum)
3) Fix typography minimums + line-height for small text (>=14px body, >=12px labels)
4) Re-audit forms and modal/drawer interactions on /booking and /contact

## Desktop breakpoint freeze (PRODUCTION-LOCKED)

- Desktop breakpoint (≥1024px) is production-locked.
- No desktop styles/layouts/spacing should be modified during responsive remediation.
- All responsive work should target tablet/mobile/large-mobile only.

## Responsive foundation primitives audit (tablet/mobile/large-mobile)

### Stack discovery (as implemented in repo)

- **Framework/runtime:** React 18 + Vite 7 (`vite.config.ts`, `src/main.tsx`)
- **Router:** `react-router-dom` (`src/main.tsx` uses `BrowserRouter`, `src/App.tsx` uses `Routes`/`Route`)
- **Styling system:** Tailwind CSS v4 + CSS custom properties tokens (`src/index.css` imports `src/styles/design-system.css` and sets Tailwind `@config`)
- **Design tokens:** `src/styles/design-system.css` (CSS variables for color/spacing/type/shadows)
- **Responsive primitives (additional):**
  - `src/styles/utility-classes.css` (`.section-shell`, `.section-padding`, `.section-padding-lg`)
  - `src/styles/responsive-layout.css` (`.responsive-container`, `.safe-area-padding`, `.nav-offset-spacer`)
- **Motion libraries:** Framer Motion (`framer-motion`), GSAP (`gsap`), Lenis (`lenis`)

### Breakpoints (exact pixel values actually used)

- **Tailwind default screens (no custom `theme.screens` found):**
  - `sm`: 640px
  - `md`: 768px
  - `lg`: 1024px
  - `xl`: 1280px
  - `2xl`: 1536px
- **CSS media queries used in code:**
  - `@media (min-width: 640px)` and `@media (max-width: 640px)` (example: `src/components/pages/TeamGrid.css`, `src/styles/responsive-layout.css`)
  - `@media (min-width: 768px)` (example: `src/styles/responsive-layout.css`)
  - `@media (min-width: 1024px)` (example: `src/styles/responsive-layout.css`)
- **JS breakpoint logic (in-use):**
  - `src/components/ui/BladeAccordion.tsx`: mobile `<768`, tablet `768–1023`, desktop `≥1024`
  - `src/hooks/useMediaQuery.ts` (`useBreakpoint`): tablet `≥768`, desktop `≥1200` (note: desktop threshold differs from Tailwind `lg`)

### Target sections (exact file paths + component names)

- **Hero section:** `src/components/ui/hero-parallax.tsx` (`HeroParallax`, `Header`) used by `src/pages/HomePage.tsx`
- **Gallery section (tattoo style images):** `src/sections/GallerySection.tsx` (`GallerySection`) used by `src/pages/HomePage.tsx`
- **Artist section (artist cards):**
  - Home page: `src/components/ui/BladeAccordion.tsx` (`BladeAccordion`) used by `src/pages/HomePage.tsx`
  - Artists page: `src/components/pages/TeamGrid.tsx` (`TeamGrid`) used by `src/pages/ArtistsPage.tsx`
- **Studio section (studio photos carousel):** `src/components/organisms/StudioCarousel.tsx` (`StudioCarousel`) used by `src/pages/HomePage.tsx`
- **Trust signals / stats cards section:**
  - Home page: `src/components/molecules/TrustSignals.tsx` (`TrustSignals`) used by `src/pages/HomePage.tsx`
  - Additional/legacy variant: `src/sections/TrustSignalsSection.tsx` (`TrustSignalsSection`)

### Breakpoint: Tablet (768px - 1023px)

**Layout Containers:**
- [ ] Flexbox/Grid primitives defined? (Partial)
- [ ] Section wrappers responsive? (Partial)
- [ ] Component stacking behavior defined? (Yes/Partial)

**Spacing System:**
- [ ] Padding tokens per breakpoint? (Yes)
- [ ] Margin/gap utilities responsive? (Partial)
- [ ] Vertical rhythm consistent? (Partial)

**Typography:**
- [ ] Heading sizes defined? (Partial)
- [ ] Body text scales? (Partial)
- [ ] Letter-spacing/line-height responsive? (Partial)

**Component Primitives:**
- [ ] Cards responsive? (Partial)
- [ ] Buttons responsive? (Partial)
- [ ] Borders/shadows responsive? (Partial)
- [ ] Overlays opacity breakpoint-aware? (Partial)

**Motion (if applicable):**
- [ ] Transitions defined? (Partial)
- [ ] Reduced-motion support? (Partial)

**Notes (tablet):**
- Token-driven section shell spacing exists via `.section-shell` / `.section-padding` / `.section-padding-lg` in `src/styles/utility-classes.css` (tablet trigger at `min-width: 768px`).
- Layout/container primitives are split across:
  - `Container.tsx` (Tailwind `sm` and `lg` only)
  - `.responsive-container` (explicit `min-width: 768px`)
  - ad-hoc section `px-*` usage in multiple components

### Breakpoint: Large-Mobile (640px - 767px)

**Layout Containers:**
- [ ] Flexbox/Grid primitives defined? (Partial)
- [ ] Section wrappers responsive? (Partial)
- [ ] Component stacking behavior defined? (Partial)

**Spacing System:**
- [ ] Padding tokens per breakpoint? (No distinct large-mobile layer)
- [ ] Margin/gap utilities responsive? (Partial)
- [ ] Vertical rhythm consistent? (Partial/Random)

**Typography:**
- [ ] Heading sizes defined? (Partial)
- [ ] Body text scales? (Mostly static)
- [ ] Letter-spacing/line-height responsive? (Mostly static)

**Component Primitives:**
- [ ] Cards responsive? (Partial)
- [ ] Buttons responsive? (Partial)
- [ ] Borders/shadows responsive? (Partial)
- [ ] Overlays opacity breakpoint-aware? (Partial)

**Motion (if applicable):**
- [ ] Transitions defined? (Partial)
- [ ] Reduced-motion support? (Partial)

**Notes (large-mobile):**
- Tailwind `sm:` (640px) is present in key primitives like `Container.tsx` (`sm:px-6`) and in multiple components.
- There is no consistently named/central “large-mobile” breakpoint layer; behavior is effectively “mobile base” + `sm:` overrides.

### Breakpoint: Mobile (0px - 639px)

**Layout Containers:**
- [ ] Flexbox/Grid primitives defined? (Partial)
- [ ] Section wrappers responsive? (Partial)
- [ ] Component stacking behavior defined? (Partial)

**Spacing System:**
- [ ] Padding tokens per breakpoint? (Yes)
- [ ] Margin/gap utilities responsive? (Partial)
- [ ] Vertical rhythm consistent? (Partial/Random)

**Typography:**
- [ ] Heading sizes defined? (Partial)
- [ ] Body text scales? (Mostly static)
- [ ] Letter-spacing/line-height responsive? (Mostly static)

**Component Primitives:**
- [ ] Cards responsive? (Partial)
- [ ] Buttons responsive? (Partial)
- [ ] Borders/shadows responsive? (Partial)
- [ ] Overlays opacity breakpoint-aware? (Partial)

**Motion (if applicable):**
- [ ] Transitions defined? (Partial)
- [ ] Reduced-motion support? (Partial)

**Notes (mobile):**
- Color tokens required by spec exist as CSS vars in `src/styles/design-system.css`:
  - `--deep-black: rgb(10 10 10)`
  - `--base-white: rgb(255 255 255)`
  - `--chrome-silver: rgb(192 192 192)`
  - `--color-text-secondary: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.8)`
- Safe-area padding primitives exist only under `@media (max-width: 640px)` in `src/styles/responsive-layout.css`.

---

## Critical gaps (top 5)

1. Large-mobile is not a first-class breakpoint layer (640–767px is handled implicitly via Tailwind `sm:` with no dedicated primitives).
2. Breakpoint definitions are inconsistent across systems (Tailwind `lg=1024` vs `useBreakpoint` in `src/hooks/useMediaQuery.ts` uses `desktop >=1200`).
3. Layout container primitives are split/inconsistent (`Container.tsx`, `.responsive-container`, and ad-hoc `max-w-* px-*` patterns all coexist).
4. Typography primitives are partially tokenized (tokens exist), but components frequently use mixed Tailwind `text-*` scales + inline `clamp()` + CSS, so per-breakpoint type behavior is inconsistent.
5. Color tokens exist, but there are still hardcoded colors/rgba usage inside components/styles (e.g., multiple components use literal `rgba(...)` / `#0a0a0a` / `bg-black`) instead of always referencing semantic CSS vars.
